[30;1m29 | [0m[35mclass F1Score(Metric):[0m
[30;1m30 | [0m[35m    """[0m
[30;1m31 | [0m[35m    F1 Score is a metric used to evaluate object detection models. It is the harmonic[0m

[30;1m33 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m34 | [0m[35m    In simple terms, F1 Score is a measure of a model's balance between precision and[0m
[30;1m35 | [0m[35m    recall (accuracy and completeness), calculated as:[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m90[0m[34m of [0m[33m157[0m[31m ]--[0m
   Rule Id: [34mBD000700[0m

   Pattern: [32m\.(request|post|get)\([0m
[30;1m394 | [0m[35m                else self._make_empty_content()[0m
[30;1m395 | [0m[35m            )[0m
[30;1m396 | [0m[35m        if self._metric_target == MetricTarget.ORIENTED_BOUNDING_BOXES:[0m
[30;1m397 | [0m[35m            obb = detections.data.get(ORIENTED_BOX_COORDINATES)[0m
[30;1m398 | [0m[35m            if obb is not None and len(obb) > 0:[0m
[30;1m399 | [0m[35m                return np.array(obb, dtype=np.float32)[0m
